<DIV align="right" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Exhibit&nbsp;10.66</B>
</DIV>


<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><B>Reduction in Named Executive Officer Salaries<BR>
and Forgoing of Bonuses</B>
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><I>Reduction in Base Salaries</I>
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Effective February&nbsp;9, 2009, the annual base salaries for each of the named executive officers
(NEOs) of Applied Materials, Inc. (&#147;Applied&#148;) have been reduced by ten percent (10%) in order to
reduce costs due to deteriorating global economic and industry conditions. This ten percent (10%)
reduction is in addition to a ten percent (10%) reduction of the NEOs&#146; annual base salaries that
was previously implemented to reduce costs. This brings the total reduction to twenty percent (20%)
below the annual base salary in effect for each NEO at this time last year. The adjusted annual
base salaries for the NEOs as of February&nbsp;9, 2009, are as follows:
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><I>NEOs to Forgo FY2009 Bonus</I>
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In support of Applied&#146;s cost-reduction activities, each of the NEOs will forgo his annual
incentive bonus for fiscal 2009, even if the performance goals related to the bonus are fully
achieved and a bonus would otherwise be payable, unless business conditions and financial results
improve significantly.
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">

<DIV align="right" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Exhibit&nbsp;10.67</B>
</DIV>


<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On March&nbsp;10, 2009, the Board of Directors (the &#147;Board&#148;) of Applied Materials, Inc. (&#147;Applied&#148;)
approved a second ten percent (10%) reduction in the annual cash retainer for non-employee
directors of the Board, in order to reduce costs in light of global economic and industry
conditions. This reduction, which became effective starting with the third quarter of fiscal year
2009, is in addition to the ten percent (10%) reduction in non-employee directors&#146; annual cash
retainer that previously was implemented in December&nbsp;2008. This brings the non-employee directors&#146;
annual cash retainer to $52,000, which is a total reduction of twenty percent (20%) from $65,000,
the annual cash retainer for non-employee directors of the Board in effect at the beginning of
Applied&#146;s 2009 fiscal year. This reduction in non-employee directors&#146; compensation is consistent
with the ongoing twenty percent (20%) reduction in base salary for each of Applied&#146;s senior
executive officers.
</DIV>


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><!-- Folio -->&nbsp;<!-- /Folio -->
</DIV>

15d-15(e)) and internal control over financial reporting (as defined in Exchange Act Rules
13a-15(f) and 15d-15(f)) for the registrant and have:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Designed such disclosure controls and procedures, or caused such disclosure controls and

relating to the registrant, including its consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to us by

</TR>

</TR>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="4%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>

reasonably likely to materially affect, the registrant&#146;s internal control over financial

</TR>

</TABLE>
